[30;1m19 | [0m[35m.. This shared-intro section is also included in docs/index.rst[0m
[30;1m20 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m21 | [0m[35mAnymail lets you send and receive email in Django using your choice[0m
[30;1m22 | [0m[35mof transactional email service providers (ESPs). It extends the[0m
[30;1m23 | [0m[35mstandard `django.core.mail` with many common ESP-added features, providing[0m
[30;1m24 | [0m[35ma consistent API that avoids locking your code to one specific ESP[0m
[30;1m25 | [0m[35m(and making it easier to change ESPs later if needed).[0m
